# PLAN.md вҖ” Implementation Roadmap and Status

**This file is the single source of implementation status.** It tells every session
what is done, in progress, blocked, and next. It **references** the
specification in `docs/architecture/` (rule R-4, AGENTS.md) and never restates it:
if you need protocol content, follow the *Spec* column.

How to work this file (full protocol: AGENTS.md):

- Sessions pick **one** milestone: the рҹ”Ё one, else the first в¬ң whose *Depends* are вң….
- A milestone is вң… only with green quality gates and a `spec-reviewer` pass without
  blockers (its *Verify* obligations are part of the milestone).
- Update this file **in the same session as the change**: status, *Current focus*,
  and a *Session log* row. Append to logs; never rewrite their history. Dates absolute
  (YYYY-MM-DD).

Legend: в¬ң pending В· рҹ”Ё in progress В· вң… done В· вӣ” blocked В· рҹ…ҝ deferred (post-v1)

---

### Track A вҖ” Protocol pallets

**Re-scoped 2026-07-14 (user-directed; see Decision log): Track A delivers production
Polkadot-SDK FRAME pallets, not frame-free models. A1вҖ“A11 are reopened в¬ң.** Their logic
already exists as **frame-free functional-core models** (state struct + `fn op(&mut self)
-> Result` + typed Event/Error + `try_state`); that code is **kept as the functional
core**, relocated to `crates/<name>-core/` (`no_std`, no `frame` deps вҖ” rule 9 / 01 В§5.2),
and preserved as the differential oracle (Python M3 вүЎ Rust core вүЎ FRAME runtime) and the
WASM-portable / auditor-consumable port. A milestone is вң… only once its pallet ships in
full FRAME production style вҖ” the **necessary parts** per pallet:

- **`crates/<name>-core/`** вҖ” the relocated frame-free model (functional core; today's
  `pallets/<name>` logic, unchanged in behavior).
- **`pallets/<name>/src/lib.rs`** вҖ” a `#[frame_support::pallet]` shell: a `Config` trait
  (`RuntimeEvent`, `WeightInfo`, constants via `Get<вҖҰ>`, `Params`/currency/asset + origin
  bounds); `#[pallet::storage]` items as `BoundedVec`/`BoundedBTreeMap` (`MaxEncodedLen`,
  bounds from 13 В§4, names + SCALE shapes matching 02 byte-for-byte вҖ” rule 5);
  `#[pallet::event]` / `#[pallet::error]` mapped 1:1 from the core; `#[pallet::call]`
  extrinsics that enforce an explicit origin (`EnsureOrigin` over `pallet-origins`, one
  SafetyFilter authority-matrix row per call вҖ” 06 В§3) then load storage вҶ’ call the core вҶ’
  persist вҶ’ deposit events, each carrying `#[pallet::weight(T::WeightInfo::вҖҰ)]`;
  `#[pallet::hooks]` with the mandatory `try_state` (15 В§1) and only the cursor-bounded
  cranks the spec allows (none where it says none вҖ” the ledger has no hooks, 03 В§10);
  `#[pallet::genesis_config]` / `genesis_build` where the pallet has genesis state.
- **`pallets/<name>/src/mock.rs`** вҖ” a mock runtime (`construct_runtime!`: `System` + the
  pallet + its dependencies, with test `Config` impls).
- **`pallets/<name>/src/tests.rs`** вҖ” per-extrinsic Г— error-path Г— origin-misuse tests
  through the closed wrapper set, limit/boundary coverage, and a `try_state` assertion
  (15 В§4.1, В§1). Audit-scope-A pallets (A1, A2, A11 вҖ” R-7) add the adversarial /
  rounding-against-the-claimant / solvency suites.
- **`pallets/<name>/src/benchmarking.rs`** + **`weights.rs`** вҖ” `#[benchmarks]` for every
  extrinsic and hook, a `WeightInfo` trait, a generated `weights.rs`, and the
  `runtime-benchmarks` feature. PoV-calibrated weights land with B5; the harness + stubs
  are part of the milestone.
- **`Cargo.toml`** вҖ” `frame-support` / `frame-system` / `frame-benchmarking` on the
  `polkadot-stable2603` pins (01 В§9), the `std` / `runtime-benchmarks` / `try-runtime`
  features, and the `<name>-core` dependency.

Scaffold via `/new-pallet` (already emits this shape); `test-engineer` authors the 15 В§4
suites; a `spec-reviewer` pass with no blockers precedes вң… (R-6). Per-pallet FRAME wrapping
lives here; runtime-level `construct_runtime!` / `impl_runtime_apis!` assembly is B1a/B2.

## Spec questions

Open ambiguities/contradictions found in `docs/architecture/`. Record them here first;
under rule R-1 a genuine defect may be corrected in the spec directly, but log
non-obvious semantic changes and confirm with the user before diverging.
Format: `| ID | Question | Spec ref | Raised | Status |`

| ID | Question | Spec ref | Raised | Status |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| SQ-219 | **15 В§4.5 names RustSec as the supply-chain mechanism, and RustSec has a demonstrated coverage gap.** В§4.5 requires "a clean `cargo-audit` (RustSec) pass"; for crates.io the GitHub Advisory Database is a strict *superset*, so an advisory can exist with no RUSTSEC id and cargo-audit is then **structurally blind** to it вҖ” not misconfigured, blind. The worked example is live: of the 25 open Dependabot alerts, `yamux 0.12.1` / **GHSA-vxx9-2994-q338 (CVE-2026-32314, HIGH** вҖ” remote unauthenticated panic, one frame) has **no RustSec counterpart at all**, so the В§4.5 gate is green and silent on it and always was. (Triage: not reached вҖ” every `sc-network` call site builds `yamux::Config::default()`, which `libp2p-yamux` maps to yamux **0.13**; the 0.12 path needs the deprecated `Config::client()`/`server()` constructors, used nowhere. Linked, never instantiated.) This session implements the minimal closure вҖ” a pinned `osv-scanner` leg gating **exactly** the complement (findings carrying no RUSTSEC id or alias), leaving everything RustSec covers to cargo-audit/`.cargo/audit.toml` so the lists never duplicate and the informational (`unmaintained`/`unsound`) classification is not lost; waivers are per-entry annotated and **expire mechanically** (a waiver matching no finding fails the gate вҖ” the SQ-155 discipline). Ratify this strengthened reading, or amend 15 В§4.5 to name RustSec **+ GHSA/OSV** as the normative advisory sources. | 15 В§4.5 (TH-34); 01 В§9 | 2026-07-17 (Dependabot alert triage) | open вҖ” mechanism implemented + gated; needs user ratification |
| SQ-172 | **No canonical `RuntimeCall` вҶ’ `[u8; 8]` resource-key mapping exists.** A8 cannot mechanically prove `Proposal.resources` equals the payload footprint (I-11). Every non-empty payload therefore fails static checks rather than trusting proposer bytes; PR #93's bot fix also rejects empty/class-less batches under 05 В§1/T4. Consequently **no payload can qualify in production** until the exhaustive bounded mapping is defined and tested by the values/classifier owner. | 05 В§1вҖ“В§2; 09 В§1.2; I-11 | 2026-07-17 (B1b compliance review; PR #93 bot fix) | resolved 2026-07-17 (B1b completion): canonical encoding defined in 05 В§1.4 (R-1 amendment, ratification requested) and implemented вҖ” tag-byte + truncated-blake2 keys, `batch_all`-only recursion, set-equality screening with the T4 taxonomy, real lock acquisition, zero-collision CI test; production payloads qualify |
| SQ-173 | **Security-prize/envelope valuation for PARAM/CODE/META is not represented on chain.** `in_cap_prize` can exactly derive TREASURY outflow, but no backing surface provides the published security prize for the other binding classes. The runtime returns `None`, blocking Adopt at decision step 9. Which pallet owns the immutable proposal-time envelope? | 05 В§5; 08 В§5.3 | 2026-07-17 (B1b compliance review) | open вҖ” fail-closed; values/classifier-envelope owner |
| SQ-174 | **Oracle value-at-risk snapshot is absent.** 07 В§6.1 requires the reporter merit bond to use a value-at-risk frozen at `Snapshot(m)`; the live vault/treasury state is mutable and cannot substitute safely. A8 returns `Balance::MAX` whenever a relevant cohort exposure exists, pricing such reports out rather than under-bonding them. | 07 В§6.1; 05 В§4.6 | 2026-07-17 (B1b compliance review) | open вҖ” fail-closed; oracle/welfare snapshot owner |
| SQ-175 | **`MetricSpec` carries no milestone target.** The MilestoneRegistry cannot normalize points or bind a frozen target for a measurement epoch. Its runtime adapter returns zero, so milestone filing/close rejects. Add the target to an authoritative versioned metric-spec surface (and reconcile 02 if exposed). | 07 В§7; 05 В§4 | 2026-07-17 (B1b compliance review) | open вҖ” fail-closed; MetricSpec schema owner |
| SQ-176 | **Three guardian powers have no downstream effect endpoint:** `pause_intake`, `activate_playbook`, and `suspend_on_gate`. The guardian core records allowance/playbook state but neither epoch nor the other Track-A pallets expose the required atomic effect/revert calls. Needs a spec decision, not a code change; the code already tracks 09. | 05 В§1.3, В§2.1 T16 vs 09 В§1.2(5); 15 I-19 | 2026-07-14 | **resolved 2026-07-14** (option a, user-approved; 05 В§1.3/В§2.1 + 15 I-19 edited вҖ” see Decision log) |

## Decision log

Spec changes and other project decisions (rule R-1, AGENTS.md).

| Date | Amendment | Authorized by | Docs touched |

| 2026-07-19 | **G0/S4 universal PARAM gate extension folded into contract v5 (R2b).** Every PARAM proposal now carries the four-book `(S,C)Г—(adopt,reject)` gate, making EVERY market-bearing class gate-bearing (predicate `PARAM \| TREASURY \| CODE \| META`). PARAM settles against the same deterministic system-wide `GateBreachFlags` facts as the other classes вҖ” a **correlated-harm proxy, not causal attribution or a claim that PARAM capture is closed** (the gate-attacking re-calibration must confirm). PARAM POL commitment 13,863 вҶ’ 34,657 USDC; runtime NAV arming floor 1,848,400 вҶ’ 4,620,989 USDC. No structural type, `gate.*`/`pol.b_gate` value, SQ-272 MIN, or `MaxLiveMarkets = 196` changed; the frozen optional-four-ID gate array + four-slot class-floor array already represent PARAM, so the semantic/value change folds into the same pre-genesis **v5** entry (no v6). Tests prove six physical PARAM books, both vetoes, AND that an honest organic-depth PARAM stays decision-grade and Adopts (the R1 reject-everything failure mode is excluded). Residual: SQ-173 (PARAM's unbacked step-9 capability-envelope prize) must land before production PARAM adoption. | User explicit directive, speaking for both backend and frontend under R-1, 2026-07-19 | 00 D-2/D-4; 01 В§3; 02 В§4/В§7/В§13; 03 В§2.1; 04 В§1.1/В§9; 05 В§4.7/В§5.1вҖ“В§5.4; 08 В§2.5/В§3вҖ“В§4.1; 13 В§1; 14 TH-4/TH-6 |

| 2026-07-18 | **SQ-272 resolution вҖ” step-9 decision-pair contest capital is the MIN of the Accept and Reject books, never their sum.** The shallower book is binding because an attacker can move the cheaper side; `b_acc + b_rej` remains summed solely for the `sec.flow_cap` ceiling. 08 В§5.4(b) pins the reading with `LМӮ = 34,657 + 400,000 = 434,657`, adding one `dec.v_min` despite both books grading individually. Runtime, reference model, generated differential vectors, and simulation are aligned; the asymmetric 400k/100k vector mutation-proves SUM would Adopt where MIN rejects. | 2026-07-18 | **`settlement_score` made exactly-rounded on both sides of the differential (G0 criterion-A defect sweep).** The 05 В§4.4(4) geometric-mean settlement score is now computed as the exact floor `isqrt(AВ·B)` in grid units in `welfare-core` (replacing an exp2/log2 path that lost 1 ulp on on-grid results; unit tests tightened from Вұ2 ulp to exact) вҖ” and the **Python reference model shared the defect class at the Оө_W corner**: its 100-digit exp2/log2 round-trip floored `settlement_with_self` at W=0 to `0` where the spec-exact value of the doubly-Оө-floored pair is exactly one base unit; fixed to the correctly-rounded `(aВ·b).sqrt()` (independent derivation, not a Rust port). Companion decide-path fixes (same sweep, no spec change вҖ” code brought to the 05 В§5.4/В§5.5 text): per-gate validity-then-veto ordering restored (a Survival veto is no longer mis-reported as `NotDecisionGrade`, which wrongly slashed 10 % of the intake bond), and a first-pass Invalid welfare grade now rejects instead of extending; both pinned by corpus rows and new pallet-epoch bond-treatment tests. | Session decisions under R-1/R-7 (spec-exact rounding; divergences were implementation bugs vs the В§5.4/В§5.5 text), user-directed G0/S4 completion drive 2026-07-18 | reference-model (`welfare.py`), corpus; Rust: welfare-core, epoch-core, pallet-epoch, pallet-market, runtime (no doc text changed) |
| 2026-07-18 | **04 В§7a accrual-grid admissibility (SQ-231 implementation follow-up).** The 10-block grid is the coarsest admissible recording for the contest-capital accumulator; a finer per-event integral is explicitly admissible (strictly conservative вҖ” only under-counts), and the literal backward interval sample MUST NOT credit a position across a boundary it did not span (a 1-block flash position would earn a full 10-block credit вҖ” the pass-widening direction). Surfaced by the runtime implementation, which uses the per-event integral the A8-remediation review had already established for the gross measure; the reference accumulator is grid-agnostic, so differential agreement is unaffected. Also: 08 В§5.4(b) gained its normative-seeding recomputation (b вүҲ 35,130; ceiling not binding at Г—7) after the reference-model implementation showed the printed floor-`b` illustration is not a configuration the В§5.3 seeding produces (ratio 8 there вҖ” the source of the Г—7-vs-8 tension, resolved in favor of Г—7 + the illustration note); 04 В§7a's marking (raw previous-block quote, USDC base-unit grid, two outcome legs) made explicit. | Session decisions under R-1 (conservative-direction codifications of the implementing sessions' findings), user-directed G0/S4 completion drive 2026-07-18 | 04, 08 |

| 2026-07-15 | A2 (#48 Codex review triage, autonomous) | Triaged the three `chatgpt-codex-connector` findings on PR #48 (`pallet-conditional-ledger`). **P1 (transactional wrapping) вҖ” FALSE POSITIVE, no fix:** Codex claimed FRAME dispatchables aren't rolled back on error unless `#[transactional]`. Added a pallet-level live-floor pre-sweep (bump `amount вҶ’ balance` when the remainder would fall in `(0, MinSplit)`) before delegating; the core's K-floor sweep is then a no-op. Added `ensure!(amount >= T::MinSplit::get())` to both Signed extrinsics (the В§5.1 rows omit it, but R-2 is the global rule; the `MarketAuthority` `do_*` paths stay exempt). Since `ledger.min_split`'s min IS the kernel floor (13 В§1), the pallet check is always вүҘ the core's, so no core/reference-model change needed. **Verification:** two regression tests (`scalar_and_gate_splits_enforce_live_min_split`, `transfer_remainder_sweep_uses_live_min_split`) drive the tunable to its 1-USDC ceiling via a now-`pub static MinSplit` mock param; confirmed both FAIL without the fixes (sweep left 0.5-USDC dust; sub-floor scalar split returned `Ok`) and pass with them. `differential_matches_frame_free_core` still green (pallet вүЎ core at the default floor).
